 sangh ke hi ek varisht netaa or vichaarkamanmohan vaidyane kaha he ki aarakshan khatm kar dena chahie

 aarakshan khatm ho or sabko samaan shiksha or samaan avasar mili'
 This is a statement like showing the firewood of the election house and it seems that the Sangh has given this statement at the feet of the BJP
 bhagwat ke is bayaan ko tab nitish kumaar ne bad-chadhakar prachaarit kiya tha
 Lalu Prasad had mentioned this in almost every speech and in this way the social engineering of the BJP that was going on among the extremely backward and Dalits was lost
 agadon ke voton tak simati bhaajapa bihar vidhansabha chunaavon main buree tarah haari
 This defeat was bjp's defeat
 lekin vishleshak maanate hai or bhaajapa ko jin kaarnon se is haar kaa saamana karnaa padaa tha, bhagwat kaa bayaan unamem se ek pramukh kaaran tha
 The bjp's equation in Uttar Pradesh The entire math of the Bharatiya Janata Party in Uttar Pradesh is around the castes that fall within the reserve
 bhaajapa ko vot kaa vishwaas keval agadon se he
 About 40 percent of the vote is such, in which the BJP hardly gets any share
 ye votbank he musalamaanon, jatvon or yadavon kaa
 The BJP cannot sit on the throne of power only with the help of the votes of the Forward
 isiilie wo apana dhyaan gair-jatav daliton or yadavon ke alaava anya obisi or ati pichhadon par kendrit kar rahi he
 The BJP estimates that the numbers needed to win can come from these caste groups
 lekin agar manmohan vaidya kaa bayaan bhaajapa virdohi dalon ke prachaar kaa naaraa ban jaataa he to bhaajapa ke liye yah ek buree khabar he
 And there is no reason that other political parties will miss this opportunity
 bhaajapa ab mushkil main he
 In a way, this is a big setback to the bjp's campaign and it can be very difficult for the BJP to ask for votes now
 bihar is tarah ke bayanon ke pratikul asar kaa pramaan he

 When the rates were set last month, the government said that the input credit that would be available to companies would not incur additional burden and would reduce costs by about 3 per cent
